(sqlite_dialect.go:11-222): SQLite-specific implementation\\n\\nEach dialect handles database-specific syntax for:\\n- Quoting identifiers\\n- Type mapping (DB_Bool, DB_Int, DB_Varchar, etc. defined in types.go:74-119)\\n- Index operations\\n- Column checks\\n- Upsert statements\\n- Table locks and unlocks\\n\\n**Migration Types (types.go:17-31, migrations.go:1-200)**: The framework supports (migrator.go:321-354), which wraps each migration in a database transaction. On error, the transaction automatically rolls back via `sess.Rollback()` (line 424), and failed migrations are logged in the migration_log table (lines 343-346) before the transaction is rolled back.\\n\\n**Migration Registration (migrations.go)**: The `OSSMigrations` struct coordinates all framework migrations, calling `AddMigration()` for each migration type in order.
